## Standard Libraries
*C++ Standard Library - including STL Containers, STL Algorithm, STL Functional, etc.*

* [C++ Standard Library](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C%2B%2B_Standard_Library) - A collection of classes and functions, which are written in the core language and part of the C++ ISO Standard itself.
* [Standard Template Library](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Template_Library) - The Standard Template Library (STL).
* [C POSIX library](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_POSIX_library) - A specification of a C standard library for POSIX systems.
* [ISO C++ Standards Committee](https://github.com/cplusplus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cplusplus?style=flat)](https://github.com/cplusplus/stargazers) - ISO/IEC JTC1/SC22/WG21 - The C++ Standards Committee. [website](http://www.open-std.org/JTC1/SC22/WG21/)
* [The GNU C Library](https://www.gnu.org/software/libc/manual) - The purpose of this manual is to tell you how to use the facilities of the GNU C Library.

## Frameworks
*C++ generic frameworks and libraries.*

* [abseil-cpp](https://github.com/abseil/abseil-cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/abseil/abseil-cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/abseil/abseil-cpp/stargazers) - Abseil C++ Common Libraries. [Apache2]
* [Apache C++ Standard Library](http://stdcxx.apache.org/) - STDCXX, A collection of algorithms, containers, iterators, and other fundamental components. [retired] [Apache2]
* [APR](http://apr.apache.org/) - Apache Portable Runtime. Another library of cross-platform utility functions. [Apache2]
* [ASL](http://stlab.adobe.com/) - Adobe Source Libraries provides peer-reviewed and portable C++ source libraries. [MIT]
* [AUI](https://github.com/aui-framework/aui) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aui-framework/aui?style=flat)](https://github.com/aui-framework/aui/stargazers) - Declarative UI toolkit for C++20. [MPL2]
* [Boost](https://github.com/boostorg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boostorg?style=flat)](https://github.com/boostorg/stargazers) :zap: - A large collection of generic C++ libraries. [Boost] [website](https://www.boost.org)
* [BDE](https://github.com/bloomberg/bde) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bloomberg/bde?style=flat)](https://github.com/bloomberg/bde/stargazers) - The BDE Development Environment from Bloomberg Labs. [Apache2]
* [C++ Workflow](https://github.com/sogou/workflow) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sogou/workflow?style=flat)](https://github.com/sogou/workflow/stargazers) :zap: - C++ Parallel Computing and Asynchronous Networking Engine. [Apache2]
* [CGraph](https://github.com/ChunelFeng/CGraph) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChunelFeng/CGraph?style=flat)](https://github.com/ChunelFeng/CGraph/stargazers) - A cross-platform DAG framework based on C++ without any 3rd-party. [MIT]
* [Cinder](https://libcinder.org/) - A community-developed, free and open source library for professional-quality creative coding. [BSD]
* [Coost](https://github.com/idealvin/coost) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/idealvin/coost?style=flat)](https://github.com/idealvin/coost/stargazers) - A tiny boost library in C++11. [MIT]
* [Cxxomfort](http://ryan.gulix.cl/fossil.cgi/cxxomfort/) - A small, header-only library that backports various facilities from more recent C++ Standards to C++03 and later. [MIT]
* [Dlib](https://github.com/davisking/dlib) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davisking/dlib?style=flat)](https://github.com/davisking/dlib/stargazers) :zap: - A toolkit for making real world machine learning and data analysis applications in C++. [Boost] [website](http://dlib.net/)
* [EASTL](https://github.com/electronicarts/EASTL) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/electronicarts/EASTL?style=flat)](https://github.com/electronicarts/EASTL/stargazers) - Electronic Arts Standard Template Library. [BSD]
* [ETL](https://github.com/ETLCPP/etl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ETLCPP/etl?style=flat)](https://github.com/ETLCPP/etl/stargazers) - Embedded Template Library. [MIT]
* [ffead-cpp](https://github.com/sumeetchhetri/ffead-cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sumeetchhetri/ffead-cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/sumeetchhetri/ffead-cpp/stargazers) - Framework for Enterprise Application Development. [Apache2]
* [Folly](https://github.com/facebook/folly) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/folly?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/folly/stargazers) - An open-source C++ library developed and used at Facebook. [Apache2]
* [FunctionalPlus](https://github.com/Dobiasd/FunctionalPlus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Dobiasd/FunctionalPlus?style=flat)](https://github.com/Dobiasd/FunctionalPlus/stargazers) - Functional Programming Library for C++. Write concise and readable C++ code. [MIT]
* [GLib](https://wiki.gnome.org/Projects/GLib) - GLib provides the core application building blocks for libraries and applications written in C. [LGPL]
* [itlib](https://github.com/iboB/itlib) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iboB/itlib?style=flat)](https://github.com/iboB/itlib/stargazers) - A collection of std-like single-header C++ libraries  [MIT]
* [JUCE](https://github.com/julianstorer/JUCE) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/julianstorer/JUCE?style=flat)](https://github.com/julianstorer/JUCE/stargazers) - An all-encompassing C++ class library for developing cross-platform software. [Core-Module: ISC, Rest: GPL2/GPL3/Proprietary] [website](http://www.juce.com/)
* [Kigs framework](https://github.com/Kigs-framework/kigs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Kigs-framework/kigs?style=flat)](https://github.com/Kigs-framework/kigs/stargazers) - A free and open source C++ modular multi-purpose cross platform RAD framework. [MIT] [website](https://kigs-framework.org/)
* [libPhenom](https://github.com/facebook/libphenom) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/libphenom?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/libphenom/stargazers) - libPhenom is an eventing framework for building high performance and high scalability systems in C. [Apache2]
* [LibSourcey](https://github.com/sourcey/libsourcey) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sourcey/libsourcey?style=flat)](https://github.com/sourcey/libsourcey/stargazers) - C++11 evented IO for real-time video streaming and high performance networking applications. [LGPL]
* [LibU](https://github.com/koanlogic/libu) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/koanlogic/libu?style=flat)](https://github.com/koanlogic/libu/stargazers) - A multiplatform utility library written in C. [BSD]
* [libxutils](https://github.com/kala13x/libxutils) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kala13x/libxutils?style=flat)](https://github.com/kala13x/libxutils/stargazers) - Simple and yet powerful cross-platform C library providing data structures, algorithms and much more. [MIT]
* [Loki](http://loki-lib.sourceforge.net/) - A C++ library of designs, containing flexible implementations of common design patterns and idioms. [MIT]
* [MiLi](https://github.com/MariadeAnton/MiLi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MariadeAnton/MiLi?style=flat)](https://github.com/MariadeAnton/MiLi/stargazers) - Minimal headers-only C++ Library. [Boost]
* [OpenFrameworks](https://github.com/openframeworks/openFrameworks) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openframeworks/openFrameworks?style=flat)](https://github.com/openframeworks/openFrameworks/stargazers) - A cross platform open source toolkit for creative coding in C++. [MIT] [website](http://www.openframeworks.cc/)
* [PhotonLibOS](https://github.com/alibaba/PhotonLibOS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alibaba/PhotonLibOS?style=flat)](https://github.com/alibaba/PhotonLibOS/stargazers) - A comprehensive C++ framework featuring efficient user-space threading (coroutine with work-stealing), I/O, networking, RPC, HTTP, etc., and used extensively in Alibaba. It is compatible with C++ 14/17/20/23, Linux, MacOS, x86-64, ARM64, gcc and clang. [Apache2] [website](https://photonlibos.github.io/)
* [Qt](https://github.com/qt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/qt?style=flat)](https://github.com/qt/stargazers) :zap: - A cross-platform application and UI framework. [GPL/LGPL/Proprietary] [website](https://www.qt.io)
* [Reason](http://code.google.com/p/reason/) - A cross platform framework designed to bring the ease of use of Java, .Net, or Python to developers who require the performance and strength of C++. [GPL2]
* [ROOT](https://root.cern.ch/) - A set of OO frameworks with all the functionality needed to handle and analyze large amounts of data in a very efficient way. Used at CERN. [LGPL]
* [rpp](https://github.com/TheNumbat/rpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TheNumbat/rpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/TheNumbat/rpp/stargazers) - Minimal Rust-inspired C++20 STL replacement. [MIT]
* [SaneCppLibraries](https://github.com/Pagghiu/SaneCppLibraries) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Pagghiu/SaneCppLibraries?style=flat)](https://github.com/Pagghiu/SaneCppLibraries/stargazers) - a set of C++ platform abstraction libraries for macOS, Windows and Linux. [MIT] [website](https://pagghiu.github.io/SaneCppLibraries/)
* [Seastar](https://github.com/scylladb/seastar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/scylladb/seastar?style=flat)](https://github.com/scylladb/seastar/stargazers) - An advanced, open-source C++ framework for high-performance server applications on modern hardware. [Apache-2.0 License] [seastar.io](http://seastar.io/)
* [sfl library](https://github.com/slavenf/sfl-library) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slavenf/sfl-library?style=flat)](https://github.com/slavenf/sfl-library/stargazers) - a header-only C++11 library that provides several new or lesser-known containers, some of which can be used in C++20 constant expressions. [zlib]
* [Siv3D](https://github.com/Siv3D/OpenSiv3D) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Siv3D/OpenSiv3D?style=flat)](https://github.com/Siv3D/OpenSiv3D/stargazers) - Siv3D (OpenSiv3D) is a C++20 framework for creative coding (2D/3D games, media art, visualizers, and simulators). [MIT] [website](https://siv3d.github.io/)
* [STLport](http://www.stlport.org/) - An exemplary version of STL. [Free]
* [STXXL](http://stxxl.sourceforge.net/) - Standard Template Library for Extra Large Data Sets. [Boost]
* [tbox](https://github.com/tboox/tbox) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tboox/tbox?style=flat)](https://github.com/tboox/tbox/stargazers) - A glib-like multi-platform c library. [Apache2] [website](http://tboox.org/)
* [Ultimate++](http://www.ultimatepp.org/) - A C++ cross-platform rapid application development framework. [BSD]
* [Windows Template Library](http://sourceforge.net/projects/wtl/) - A C++ library for developing Windows applications and UI components. [Public]
* [WUI](https://github.com/intent-garden/wui) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/intent-garden/wui?style=flat)](https://github.com/intent-garden/wui/stargazers) - WUI (Window User Interface Library) is a cross-platform library for creating graphical user interfaces in C++17+ [Boost][website](https://libwui.org)
* [xtd](https://github.com/gammasoft71/xtd) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gammasoft71/xtd?style=flat)](https://github.com/gammasoft71/xtd/stargazers) - Modern C++20 framework to create console (CLI), forms (GUI) and unit tests (xUnit) applications on Windows, macOS, Linux, iOS, Android, FreeBSD and Haiku. [MIT]
* [Yomm2](https://github.com/jll63/yomm2) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jll63/yomm2?style=flat)](https://github.com/jll63/yomm2/stargazers) - Fast, Orthogonal, Open multi-methods. Supersedes [Yomm11](https://github.com/jll63/yomm11) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jll63/yomm11?style=flat)](https://github.com/jll63/yomm11/stargazers) [Boost]

## Artificial Intelligence

* [ANNetGPGPU](https://github.com/ANNetGPGPU/ANNetGPGPU) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ANNetGPGPU/ANNetGPGPU?style=flat)](https://github.com/ANNetGPGPU/ANNetGPGPU/stargazers) - A GPU (CUDA) based Artificial Neural Network library. [LGPL]
* [btsk](https://github.com/aigamedev/btsk) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aigamedev/btsk?style=flat)](https://github.com/aigamedev/btsk/stargazers) - Game Behavior Tree Starter Kit. [zlib]
* [cpp-mcp](https://github.com/hkr04/cpp-mcp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hkr04/cpp-mcp?style=flat)](https://github.com/hkr04/cpp-mcp/stargazers) - Lightweight C++ MCP (Model Context Protocol) SDK. [MIT]
* [Evolving Objects](http://eodev.sourceforge.net/) - A template-based, ANSI-C++ evolutionary computation library which helps you to write your own stochastic optimization algorithms insanely fast. [LGPL]
* [fastmcpp](https://github.com/0xeb/fastmcpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/0xeb/fastmcpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/0xeb/fastmcpp/stargazers) - C++ port of the fastmcp Python library. [Apache2]
* [frugally-deep](https://github.com/Dobiasd/frugally-deep) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Dobiasd/frugally-deep?style=flat)](https://github.com/Dobiasd/frugally-deep/stargazers) - Header-only library for using Keras models in C++. [MIT]
* [Genann](https://github.com/codeplea/genann) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codeplea/genann?style=flat)](https://github.com/codeplea/genann/stargazers) - Simple neural network library in C. [zlib]
* [MXNet](https://github.com/apache/incubator-mxnet) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apache/incubator-mxnet?style=flat)](https://github.com/apache/incubator-mxnet/stargazers) - Lightweight, Portable, Flexible Distributed/Mobile Deep Learning with Dynamic, Mutation-aware Dataflow Dep Scheduler; for Python, R, Julia, Scala, Go, JavaScript and more. [website](https://mxnet.apache.org)
* [PyTorch](https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pytorch/pytorch?style=flat)](https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/stargazers) - Tensors and Dynamic neural networks in Python with strong GPU acceleration. [website](https://pytorch.org)
* [flashlight](https://github.com/flashlight/flashlight) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flashlight/flashlight?style=flat)](https://github.com/flashlight/flashlight/stargazers) - Flashlight is a fast, flexible machine learning library written entirely in C++. [BSD]
* [Recast/Detour](https://github.com/recastnavigation/recastnavigation) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/recastnavigation/recastnavigation?style=flat)](https://github.com/recastnavigation/recastnavigation/stargazers) - (3D) Navigation mesh generator and pathfinder, mostly for games. [zlib]
* [TensorFlow](https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tensorflow/tensorflow?style=flat)](https://github.com/tensorflow/tensorflow/stargazers) - An open source software library for numerical computation using data flow graphs. [Apache]
* [Txeo](https://github.com/rdabra/txeo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rdabra/txeo?style=flat)](https://github.com/rdabra/txeo/stargazers) - A modern C++ wrapper for TensorFlow. [Apache]
* [oneDNN](https://github.com/oneapi-src/oneDNN) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oneapi-src/oneDNN?style=flat)](https://github.com/oneapi-src/oneDNN/stargazers) - An open-source cross-platform performance library for deep learning applications. [Apache] [website](https://01.org/onednn)
* [CNTK](https://github.com/Microsoft/CNTK) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Microsoft/CNTK?style=flat)](https://github.com/Microsoft/CNTK/stargazers) - Microsoft Cognitive Toolkit (CNTK), an open source deep-learning toolkit. [Boost]
* [tiny-dnn](https://github.com/tiny-dnn/tiny-dnn) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tiny-dnn/tiny-dnn?style=flat)](https://github.com/tiny-dnn/tiny-dnn/stargazers) - A header only, dependency-free deep learning framework in C++11. [BSD]
* [Veles](https://github.com/Samsung/veles) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Samsung/veles?style=flat)](https://github.com/Samsung/veles/stargazers) - Distributed platform for rapid Deep learning application development. [Apache]
* [Kaldi](https://github.com/kaldi-asr/kaldi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kaldi-asr/kaldi?style=flat)](https://github.com/kaldi-asr/kaldi/stargazers) - Toolkit for speech recognition. [Apache]

## Asynchronous Event Loop

* [Asio](https://github.com/chriskohlhoff/asio/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chriskohlhoff/asio/?style=flat)](https://github.com/chriskohlhoff/asio//stargazers) - A cross-platform C++ library for network and low-level I/O programming that provides developers with a consistent asynchronous model using a modern C++ approach. [Boost] [website](http://think-async.com/)
* [Boost.Asio](https://github.com/boostorg/asio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boostorg/asio?style=flat)](https://github.com/boostorg/asio/stargazers) - A cross-platform C++ library for network and low-level I/O programming. [Boost] [website](https://boost.org/libs/asio)
* [C++ Actor Framework](https://github.com/actor-framework/actor-framework) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/actor-framework/actor-framework?style=flat)](https://github.com/actor-framework/actor-framework/stargazers) - An Open Source Implementation of the Actor Model in C++. [BSD-3-Clause] [website](http://actor-framework.org/)
* [Ichor](https://github.com/volt-software/ichor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/volt-software/ichor?style=flat)](https://github.com/volt-software/ichor/stargazers) - An event queue which focuses on thread safety and provides dependency injection. [MIT]
* [libev](http://libev.schmorp.de/) - A full-featured and high-performance event loop that is loosely modelled after libevent, but without its limitations and bugs. [BSD and GPL]
* [libevent](http://libevent.org/) - An event notification library. [BSD]
* [libhv](https://github.com/ithewei/libhv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ithewei/libhv?style=flat)](https://github.com/ithewei/libhv/stargazers) - Cross-platform event loop library. [BSD]
* [libuv](https://github.com/libuv/libuv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/libuv/libuv?style=flat)](https://github.com/libuv/libuv/stargazers) - Cross-platform asynchronous I/O. [BSD]
* [promise-cpp](https://github.com/xhawk18/promise-cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xhawk18/promise-cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/xhawk18/promise-cpp/stargazers) - Header only library that implements Promise/A+ standard. [Anti-996]
* [uvw](https://github.com/skypjack/uvw) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skypjack/uvw?style=flat)](https://github.com/skypjack/uvw/stargazers) - C++ wrapper for libuv. [MIT]
* [uv-cpp](https://github.com/wlgq2/uv-cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wlgq2/uv-cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/wlgq2/uv-cpp/stargazers) - a simple interface, high-performance network library based on C++11. [MIT]

## Audio
*Audio, Sound, Music, Digitized Voice Libraries*

* [Amplitude Audio SDK](https://github.com/SparkyStudios/AmplitudeAudioSDK) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SparkyStudios/AmplitudeAudioSDK?style=flat)](https://github.com/SparkyStudios/AmplitudeAudioSDK/stargazers) - A cross-platform audio engine designed with the needs of games in mind. [Apache-2.0] [website](https://amplitudeaudiosdk.com)

[GPL] [website](https://github.com/m-a-d-n-e-s-s/madness) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m-a-d-n-e-s-s/madness?style=flat)](https://github.com/m-a-d-n-e-s-s/madness/stargazers)

## Compression
*Compression and Archiving Libraries*

* [bit7z](https://github.com/rikyoz/bit7z) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rikyoz/bit7z?style=flat)](https://github.com/rikyoz/bit7z/stargazers) - A C++ static library offering a clean and simple interface to the 7-zip shared libraries. [MPL2]
* [Brotli](https://github.com/google/brotli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/brotli?style=flat)](https://github.com/google/brotli/stargazers) - Brotli compression format. Developed by Google. [MIT]
* [bzip2](http://www.bzip.org/) - A freely available, patent free, high-quality data compressor. [BSD]
* [bzip3](https://github.com/kspalaiologos/bzip3) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kspalaiologos/bzip3?style=flat)](https://github.com/kspalaiologos/bzip3/stargazers) - A better and stronger spiritual successor to BZip2. [LGPL]
* [FastLZ](https://github.com/ariya/FastLZ) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ariya/FastLZ?style=flat)](https://github.com/ariya/FastLZ/stargazers) - Small & portable byte-aligned LZ77 compression. [MIT]
* [FiniteStateEntropy](https://github.com/Cyan4973/FiniteStateEntropy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyan4973/FiniteStateEntropy?style=flat)](https://github.com/Cyan4973/FiniteStateEntropy/stargazers) - New generation entropy codecs : Finite State Entropy and Huff0.
* [FSST](https://github.com/cwida/fsst) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cwida/fsst?style=flat)](https://github.com/cwida/fsst/stargazers) - efficient random-access string compression. [MIT]
* [heatshrink](https://github.com/atomicobject/heatshrink) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/atomicobject/heatshrink?style=flat)](https://github.com/atomicobject/heatshrink/stargazers) - data compression library for embedded/real-time systems  [ISC]
* [Kanzi](https://github.com/flanglet/kanzi-cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flanglet/kanzi-cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/flanglet/kanzi-cpp/stargazers) - a modern, modular, portable and efficient lossless data compressor implemented in C++. [Apache-2.0]
* [KArchive](https://api.kde.org/frameworks/karchive/html/index.html) - A library for creating, reading, writing and manipulating file archives like zip and tar. It also provides transparent compression and decompression of data, using formats like gzip, via a subclass of QIODevice. [LGPL]
* [libarchive](https://github.com/libarchive/libarchive) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/libarchive/libarchive?style=flat)](https://github.com/libarchive/libarchive/stargazers) - Multi-format archive and compression library. [New BSD] [website](http://www.libarchive.org/)
* [LZ4](https://github.com/lz4/lz4) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lz4/lz4?style=flat)](https://github.com/lz4/lz4/stargazers) - Extremely Fast Compression algorithm. [BSD] [website](http://www.lz4.org/)
* [LZAV](https://github.com/avaneev/lzav) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/avaneev/lzav?style=flat)](https://github.com/avaneev/lzav/stargazers) - Fast In-Memory Data Compression Algorithm. [MIT]
* [LZFSE](https://github.com/lzfse/lzfse) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lzfse/lzfse?style=flat)](https://github.com/lzfse/lzfse/stargazers) - LZFSE compression library and command line tool. Developed by Apple.
* [LZHAM](https://code.google.com/p/lzham/) - Lossless data compression library with a compression ratio similar to LZMA but with much faster decompression. [BSD]
* [LZMA](https://sourceforge.net/projects/sevenzip/files/7-Zip) :zap: - The default and general compression method of 7z format. [PublicDomain] [website](https://www.7-zip.org)
* [LZMAT](http://www.matcode.com/lzmat.htm) - An extremely fast real-time lossless data compression library. [GPL]
* [miniz](https://github.com/richgel999/miniz) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/richgel999/miniz?style=flat)](https://github.com/richgel999/miniz/stargazers) - Single C source file Deflate/Inflate compression library with zlib-compatible API, ZIP archive reading/writing, PNG writing. [MIT]
* [Minizip](https://github.com/nmoinvaz/minizip) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nmoinvaz/minizip?style=flat)](https://github.com/nmoinvaz/minizip/stargazers) - Zlib with latest bug fixes that supports PKWARE disk spanning, AES encryption, and IO buffering. [zlib]
* [minizip-ng](https://github.com/zlib-ng/minizip-ng) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zlib-ng/minizip-ng?style=flat)](https://github.com/zlib-ng/minizip-ng/stargazers) - Fork of the popular zip manipulation library found in the zlib distribution. [zlib]
* [OpenZL](https://github.com/facebook/openzl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/openzl?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/openzl/stargazers) - A novel data compression framework. [BSD] [website](https://openzl.org/)
* [PhysicsFS](https://icculus.org/physfs/) - A library to provide abstract access to various archives. It is intended for use in video games, and the design was somewhat inspired by Quake 3's file subsystem. [zlib]
* [Rapidgzip](https://github.com/mxmlnkn/rapidgzip) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mxmlnkn/rapidgzip?style=flat)](https://github.com/mxmlnkn/rapidgzip/stargazers) - Gzip Decompression and Random Access for Modern Multi-Core Machines. [Apache-2/MIT]
* [smaz](https://github.com/antirez/smaz) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antirez/smaz?style=flat)](https://github.com/antirez/smaz/stargazers) - Small strings compression library. [BSD]
* [Snappy](https://google.github.io/snappy/) - A fast compressor/decompressor. [BSD]
* [ZLib](http://zlib.net/) - A very compact compression library for data streams. [zlib]
* [zlib-ng](https://github.com/zlib-ng/zlib-ng) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zlib-ng/zlib-ng?style=flat)](https://github.com/zlib-ng/zlib-ng/stargazers) - zlib for the "next generation" systems. Drop-In replacement with some serious optimizations. [zlib]
* [zstd](https://github.com/facebook/zstd) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/zstd?style=flat)](https://github.com/facebook/zstd/stargazers) - Zstandard - Fast real-time compression algorithm. Developed by Facebook. [BSD]
* [ZXC](https://github.com/hellobertrand/zxc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hellobertrand/zxc?style=flat)](https://github.com/hellobertrand/zxc/stargazers) - High-performance asymmetric lossless compression. [BSD-3-Clause]
* [ZZIPlib](http://zziplib.sourceforge.net/) - Provides read access on ZIP-archives. [MPL/LGPL]
* [cmix](https://github.com/byronknoll/cmix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/byronknoll/cmix?style=flat)](https://github.com/byronknoll/cmix/stargazers) - A lossless data compression program that aims for the highest compression ratios at the cost of speed. [GPL-3.0]
* [LZSSE-SIMDe](https://github.com/nemequ/LZSSE-SIMDe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nemequ/LZSSE-SIMDe?style=flat)](https://github.com/nemequ/LZSSE-SIMDe/stargazers) - A portable SIMD implementation of LZSSE compression. [BSD-2-Clause]
* [Zopfli](https://github.com/google/zopfli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/zopfli?style=flat)](https://github.com/google/zopfli/stargazers) - A compression library that performs very good but slow deflate/zlib compression. [Apache-2.0]

* [hat-trie](https://github.com/Tessil/hat-trie) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Tessil/hat-trie?style=flat)](https://github.com/Tessil/hat-trie/stargazers) - C++ implementation of a fast and memory efficient HAT-trie. [MIT]
* [Hopscotch map](https://github.com/Tessil/hopscotch-map) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Tessil/hopscotch-map?style=flat)](https://github.com/Tessil/hopscotch-map/stargazers) - A fast header-only hash map which uses hopscotch hashing for collisions resolution. [MIT]
* [librb](https://github.com/mlyszczek/librb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mlyszczek/librb?style=flat)](https://github.com/mlyszczek/librb/stargazers) - C implementation of ring (circular) buffer, with full thread awareness that allows for concurrent read/write and can automatically grow in size when needed. [BSD] [website](https://librb.bofc.pl/)
* [LSHBOX](https://github.com/RSIA-LIESMARS-WHU/LSHBOX) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RSIA-LIESMARS-WHU/LSHBOX?style=flat)](https://github.com/RSIA-LIESMARS-WHU/LSHBOX/stargazers) - A c++ toolbox of locality-sensitive hashing (LSH), provides several popular LSH algorithms, also support Python and MATLAB. [GPL]
* [marisa-trie](https://github.com/s-yata/marisa-trie) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/s-yata/marisa-trie?style=flat)](https://github.com/s-yata/marisa-trie/stargazers) - Matching Algorithm with Recursively Implemented StorAge. [BSD-2-Clause/LGPL-2.1]
* [parallel-hashmap](https://github.com/greg7mdp/parallel-hashmap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/greg7mdp/parallel-hashmap?style=flat)](https://github.com/greg7mdp/parallel-hashmap/stargazers) - A family of header-only, very fast and memory-friendly hashmap and btree containers [Apache2] [website](https://greg7mdp.github.io/parallel-hashmap/)
* [PGM-index](https://github.com/gvinciguerra/PGM-index) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gvinciguerra/PGM-index?style=flat)](https://github.com/gvinciguerra/PGM-index/stargazers) - A data structure that enables fast lookup, predecessor, range searches and updates in arrays of billions of items using orders of magnitude less space than traditional indexes. [Apache2] [website](https://pgm.di.unipi.it)
* [plf::colony](https://github.com/mattreecebentley/plf_colony) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattreecebentley/plf_colony?style=flat)](https://github.com/mattreecebentley/plf_colony/stargazers) - An unordered "bag"-type container which outperforms std containers in high-modification scenarios while maintaining permanent pointers to non-erased elements regardless of insertion/erasure. [zLib] [website](http://www.plflib.org/colony.htm)
* [plf::list](https://github.com/mattreecebentley/plf_list) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattreecebentley/plf_list?style=flat)](https://github.com/mattreecebentley/plf_list/stargazers) - A std::list implementation which removes range splicing in order to enable cache-friendlier structure, yielding significant performance gains. [zLib] [website](http://www.plflib.org/list.htm)
* [plf::stack](https://github.com/mattreecebentley/plf_stack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattreecebentley/plf_stack?style=flat)](https://github.com/mattreecebentley/plf_stack/stargazers) - A replacement container for the std::stack container adaptor, with better performance than any std container in a stack context. [zLib] [website](http://www.plflib.org/stack.htm)
* [ring_span lite](https://github.com/martinmoene/ring-span-lite) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/martinmoene/ring-span-lite?style=flat)](https://github.com/martinmoene/ring-span-lite/stargazers) - A simplified implementation of Arthur O'Dwyer's ring_span implementation ie. a circular buffer view. [MIT]
* [robin-hood-hashing](https://github.com/martinus/robin-hood-hashing) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/martinus/robin-hood-hashing?style=flat)](https://github.com/martinus/robin-hood-hashing/stargazers) - Fast & memory efficient hashtable based on robin hood hashing for C++14. [MIT]
* [robin-map](https://github.com/Tessil/robin-map) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Tessil/robin-map?style=flat)](https://github.com/Tessil/robin-map/stargazers) - Fast hash map and hash set using robin hood hashing. [MIT]
* [sparsepp](https://github.com/greg7mdp/sparsepp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/greg7mdp/sparsepp?style=flat)](https://github.com/greg7mdp/sparsepp/stargazers) - A fast, memory efficient hash map for C++. [BSD 3-clause]
* [sqlitemap](https://github.com/bw-hro/sqlitemap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bw-hro/sqlitemap?style=flat)](https://github.com/bw-hro/sqlitemap/stargazers) - Persistent map backed by SQLite. [MIT]
* [st_tree](https://github.com/erikerlandson/st_tree) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/erikerlandson/st_tree?style=flat)](https://github.com/erikerlandson/st_tree/stargazers) - A fast and flexible c++ template class for tree data structures. [Apache-2.0]
* [svector](https://github.com/martinus/svector) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/martinus/svector?style=flat)](https://github.com/martinus/svector/stargazers) - Compact SVO optimized vector for C++17 or higher. [MIT]
* [tree.hh](https://github.com/kpeeters/tree.hh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kpeeters/tree.hh?style=flat)](https://github.com/kpeeters/tree.hh/stargazers) - An STL-like C++ header-only tree library. [GPL2+]
* [unordered_dense](https://github.com/martinus/unordered_dense) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/martinus/unordered_dense?style=flat)](https://github.com/martinus/unordered_dense/stargazers) - A fast & densely stored hashmap and hashset based on robin-hood backward shift deletion. [MIT]
* [fifo_map](https://github.com/nlohmann/fifo_map) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nlohmann/fifo_map?style=flat)](https://github.com/nlohmann/fifo_map/stargazers) - A FIFO-ordered associative container for C++. [MIT]
* [ordered-map](https://github.com/Tessil/ordered-map) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Tessil/ordered-map?style=flat)](https://github.com/Tessil/ordered-map/stargazers) - A C++ hash map and hash set which preserves the order of insertion. [MIT]

## Cryptography
*Cryptography and Encryption Libraries*

* [Bcrypt](http://bcrypt.sourceforge.net/) - A cross platform file encryption utility. Encrypted files are portable across all supported operating systems and processors. [BSD]
* [BeeCrypt](http://beecrypt.sourceforge.net/) - A portable and fast cryptography library. [LGPLv2.1+]
* [Botan](http://botan.randombit.net/) - A crypto library for C++. [BSD-2]
* [Crypto++](https://github.com/weidai11/cryptopp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/weidai11/cryptopp?style=flat)](https://github.com/weidai11/cryptopp/stargazers) - A free C++ class library of cryptographic schemes. [Boost] [website](http://www.cryptopp.com/)
* [digestpp](https://github.com/kerukuro/digestpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kerukuro/digestpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/kerukuro/digestpp/stargazers) - C++11 header-only message digest (hash) library. [PublicDomain]
* [GnuPG](https://www.gnupg.org/) - A complete and free implementation of the OpenPGP standard. [GPL]
* [GnuTLS](http://www.gnutls.org/) - A secure communications library implementing the SSL, TLS and DTLS protocols. [LGPL2.1]
* [Libgcrypt](http://www.gnu.org/software/libgcrypt/) - A general purpose cryptographic library originally based on code from GnuPG. [LGPLv2.1+]
* [LibreSSL](http://www.libressl.org/) - A free version of the SSL/TLS protocol forked from OpenSSL in 2014. [?]
* [libsodium](https://github.com/jedisct1/libsodium) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jedisct1/libsodium?style=flat)](https://github.com/jedisct1/libsodium/stargazers) - P(ortable|ackageable) NaCl-based crypto library, opinionated and easy to use. [ISC]
* [libhydrogen](https://github.com/jedisct1/libhydrogen) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jedisct1/libhydrogen?style=flat)](https://github.com/jedisct1/libhydrogen/stargazers) - A lightweight, secure, easy-to-use crypto library suitable for constrained environments. [ISC]
* [LibTomCrypt](https://github.com/libtom/libtomcrypt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/libtom/libtomcrypt?style=flat)](https://github.com/libtom/libtomcrypt/stargazers) - A fairly comprehensive, modular and portable cryptographic toolkit. [WTFPL]
* [mbedTLS](https://github.com/ARMmbed/mbedtls) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ARMmbed/mbedtls?style=flat)](https://github.com/ARMmbed/mbedtls/stargazers) - An open source, portable, easy to use, readable and flexible SSL library, previously known as PolarSSL. [Apache2] [website](https://tls.mbed.org/)
* [Nettle](http://www.lysator.liu.se/~nisse/nettle/) - A low-level cryptographic library. [LGPL]
* [OpenSSL](https://github.com/openssl/openssl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openssl/openssl?style=flat)](https://github.com/openssl/openssl/stargazers) - A robust, commercial-grade, full-featured, and Open Source cryptography library. [Apache] [website](http://www.openssl.org/)
* [retter](https://github.com/MaciejCzyzewski/retter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MaciejCzyzewski/retter?style=flat)](https://github.com/MaciejCzyzewski/retter/stargazers) - A collection of hash functions, ciphers, tools, libraries, and materials related to cryptography.
* [s2n](https://github.com/awslabs/s2n) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awslabs/s2n?style=flat)](https://github.com/awslabs/s2n/stargazers) - An implementation of the TLS/SSL protocols. [Apache]
* [sha1collisiondetection](https://github.com/cr-marcstevens/sha1collisiondetection) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cr-marcstevens/sha1collisiondetection?style=flat)](https://github.com/cr-marcstevens/sha1collisiondetection/stargazers) - Library and command line tool to detect SHA-1 collision in a file. [MIT]
* [stduuid](https://github.com/mariusbancila/stduuid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mariusbancila/stduuid?style=flat)](https://github.com/mariusbancila/stduuid/stargazers) - A C++17 cross-platform implementation for UUIDs. [MIT]
* [Tink](https://github.com/google/tink) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/tink?style=flat)](https://github.com/google/tink/stargazers) - A multi-language, cross-platform library that provides cryptographic APIs that are secure, easy to use correctly, and hard(er) to misuse. [Apache-2.0]
* [Tiny AES in C](https://github.com/kokke/tiny-AES-c) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kokke/tiny-AES-c?style=flat)](https://github.com/kokke/tiny-AES-c/stargazers) - Small portable AES128/192/256 in C. [PublicDomain]
* [tiny-ECDH-c](https://github.com/kokke/tiny-ECDH-c) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kokke/tiny-ECDH-c?style=flat)](https://github.com/kokke/tiny-ECDH-c/stargazers) - Small and portable implementation of the ECDH key agreement protocol in C. [PublicDomain]
* [Themis](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cossacklabs/themis?style=flat)](https://github.com/cossacklabs/themis/stargazers) - crypto library for painless data security, providing symmetric and asymmetric encryption, secure sockets with forward secrecy, for mobile and server platforms. [Apache2]
* [HEhub](https://github.com/primihub/HEhub) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/primihub/HEhub?style=flat)](https://github.com/primihub/HEhub/stargazers) - A library for homomorphic encryption and its applications. [Apache2]
* [Qt-Secret](https://github.com/QuasarApp/Qt-Secret) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/QuasarApp/Qt-Secret?style=flat)](https://github.com/QuasarApp/Qt-Secret/stargazers) - Simple encryption library based on Qt for C++ projects. [LGPL]
* [micro-ecc](https://github.com/kmackay/micro-ecc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kmackay/micro-ecc?style=flat)](https://github.com/kmackay/micro-ecc/stargazers) - A small and fast ECDH and ECDSA implementation for 8-bit, 32-bit, and 64-bit processors. [BSD-2-Clause]
* [crypto-algorithms](https://github.com/B-Con/crypto-algorithms) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/B-Con/crypto-algorithms?style=flat)](https://github.com/B-Con/crypto-algorithms/stargazers) - Basic implementations of standard cryptography algorithms (AES, SHA, etc.) in C. [PublicDomain]
* [aes-stream](https://github.com/jedisct1/aes-stream) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jedisct1/aes-stream?style=flat)](https://github.com/jedisct1/aes-stream/stargazers) - A fast AES-based stream cipher for C. [ISC]

* [SQLite](http://www.sqlite.org/) - A completely embedded, full-featured relational database in a few 100k that you can include right into your project. [PublicDomain]
* [SQLiteC++](https://github.com/SRombauts/SQLiteCpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SRombauts/SQLiteCpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/SRombauts/SQLiteCpp/stargazers) - SQLiteC++ (SQLiteCpp) is a smart and easy to use C++ SQLite3 wrapper. [MIT]

* [otfcc](https://github.com/caryll/otfcc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/caryll/otfcc?style=flat)](https://github.com/caryll/otfcc/stargazers) - A C library and utility used for parsing and writing OpenType font files. [Apache-2.0]
* [harfbuzz](https://github.com/harfbuzz/harfbuzz) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/harfbuzz/harfbuzz?style=flat)](https://github.com/harfbuzz/harfbuzz/stargazers) - A text shaping engine. [Old MIT]
* [libschrift](https://github.com/tomolt/libschrift) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomolt/libschrift?style=flat)](https://github.com/tomolt/libschrift/stargazers) - A lightweight TrueType font rendering library. [ISC]
* [SheenBidi](https://github.com/Tehreer/SheenBidi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Tehreer/SheenBidi?style=flat)](https://github.com/Tehreer/SheenBidi/stargazers) - A sophisticated implementation of Unicode Bidirectional Algorithm. [Apache-2.0]

## Game Engine

[MIT]

[Apache-2.0 license]

## Graphics

* [assimp](https://github.com/assimp/assimp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/assimp/assimp?style=flat)](https://github.com/assimp/assimp/stargazers) - Open Asset Import Library (assimp) is a cross-platform 3D model import library which aims to provide a common API for different 3D asset file formats. [BSD-3-Clause] [website](http://www.assimp.org)
* [bgfx](https://github.com/bkaradzic/bgfx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bkaradzic/bgfx?style=flat)](https://github.com/bkaradzic/bgfx/stargazers) - A cross-platform rendering library. [BSD]

* [C-Turtle](https://github.com/walkerje/C-Turtle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/walkerje/C-Turtle?style=flat)](https://github.com/walkerje/C-Turtle/stargazers) - A C++11 header-only turtle graphics library acting as a CImg wrapper. [MIT]

* [Harfang 3D](https://github.com/harfang3d/harfang3d) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/harfang3d/harfang3d?style=flat)](https://github.com/harfang3d/harfang3d/stargazers) 3D visualization library usable in C++, Python, Lua and Go. * [Horde3D](https://github.com/horde3d/Horde3D) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/horde3d/Horde3D?style=flat)](https://github.com/horde3d/Horde3D/stargazers) - A small 3D rendering and animation engine. [EPL]

* [Irrlicht](http://irrlicht.sourceforge.net/) - A high performance realtime 3D engine written in C++. [zlib]
* [libigl](https://github.com/libigl/libigl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/libigl/libigl?style=flat)](https://github.com/libigl/libigl/stargazers) - Simple C++ geometry processing library. [MPL2]
* [LLGL](https://github.com/LukasBanana/LLGL) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LukasBanana/LLGL?style=flat)](https://github.com/LukasBanana/LLGL/stargazers) - Low Level Graphics Library (LLGL) is a thin abstraction layer for the modern graphics APIs. [BSD-3-Clause]
* [LunaSVG](https://github.com/sammycage/lunasvg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sammycage/lunasvg?style=flat)](https://github.com/sammycage/lunasvg/stargazers) - a standalone SVG rendering library in C++. [MIT]

* [micro-gl](https://github.com/micro-gl/micro-gl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/micro-gl/micro-gl?style=flat)](https://github.com/micro-gl/micro-gl/stargazers) - Realtime, Embeddable, Headers Only C++11 CPU vector graphics. no STD lib, no FPU and no GPU required. [CUSTOM] [website](https://micro-gl.github.io/docs/microgl)
* [NanoVG](https://github.com/memononen/nanovg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/memononen/nanovg?style=flat)](https://github.com/memononen/nanovg/stargazers) - Antialiased 2D vector drawing library on top of OpenGL for UI and visualizations. [Zlib]
* [Ogre 3D](https://github.com/OGRECave) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/OGRECave?style=flat)](https://github.com/OGRECave/stargazers) :zap: - A scene-oriented, real-time, flexible 3D rendering engine (as opposed to a game engine) written in C++. [MIT] [website](https://www.ogre3d.org)
* [OpenSceneGraph](http://www.openscenegraph.org/) - An open source high performance 3D graphics toolkit. [OSGPL]
* [OpenSubdiv](https://github.com/PixarAnimationStudios/OpenSubdiv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PixarAnimationStudios/OpenSubdiv?style=flat)](https://github.com/PixarAnimationStudios/OpenSubdiv/stargazers) - Pixar's library for evaluating and rendering subdivision surfaces on CPU and GPU. [Modified Apache2]
* [OpenVDB](http://www.openvdb.org/) - Library and tools for storing, editing, and rendering volumetric datasets. [MPL2]
* [Panda3D](http://www.panda3d.org/) - A framework for 3D rendering and game development for Python and C++. [BSD]
* [Partio](https://github.com/wdas/partio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wdas/partio?style=flat)](https://github.com/wdas/partio/stargazers) - Library for wrangling particle data, with support for most common file formats. [Modified BSD]
* [Skia](https://github.com/google/skia) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/skia?style=flat)](https://github.com/google/skia/stargazers) - A complete 2D graphic library for drawing Text, Geometries, and Images. [BSD] [website](https://skia.org/)
* [ThorVG](https://github.com/thorvg/thorvg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thorvg/thorvg?style=flat)](https://github.com/thorvg/thorvg/stargazers) - a platform-independent portable library that allows for drawing vector-based scenes and animations, including SVG and Lottie. [MIT] [website](https://www.thorvg.org/)
* [TinySpline](https://github.com/msteinbeck/tinyspline) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/msteinbeck/tinyspline?style=flat)](https://github.com/msteinbeck/tinyspline/stargazers) - A small, yet powerful ANSI C library for interpolating, transforming, and querying arbitrary NURBS, B-Splines, and Bézier curves. [MIT]
* [urho3d](https://github.com/urho3d/Urho3D) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/urho3d/Urho3D?style=flat)](https://github.com/urho3d/Urho3D/stargazers) - Cross-platform rendering and game engine. [Many different, mostly MIT]
* [Yocto/GL](https://github.com/xelatihy/yocto-gl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xelatihy/yocto-gl?style=flat)](https://github.com/xelatihy/yocto-gl/stargazers) - Tiny C++ Libraries for Data-Driven Physically-based Graphics. [MIT]
* [olive.c](https://github.com/tsoding/olive.c) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tsoding/olive.c?style=flat)](https://github.com/tsoding/olive.c/stargazers) - Simple 2D Graphics Library. [MIT]

## Image Processing

* [avir](https://github.com/avaneev/avir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/avaneev/avir?style=flat)](https://github.com/avaneev/avir/stargazers) - High-quality Pro HDR image resizer and fast SIMD Lanczos resizer. [MIT]
* [Boost.GIL](https://github.com/boostorg/gil) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boostorg/gil?style=flat)](https://github.com/boostorg/gil/stargazers) - Generic Image Library. [Boost] [website](https://boost.org/libs/gil)
* [BitmapPlusPLus](https://github.com/baderouaich/BitmapPlusPlus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/baderouaich/BitmapPlusPlus?style=flat)](https://github.com/baderouaich/BitmapPlusPlus/stargazers) - Simple and Fast header only Bitmap C++ library. [MIT]
* [CImg](http://cimg.eu/) - A small, open source, C++ toolkit for image processing. [Own LGPL or GPL]
* [CxImage](https://www.codeproject.com/Articles/1300/CxImage) - An image processing and conversion library to load, save, display, transform BMP, JPEG, GIF, PNG, TIFF, MNG, ICO, PCX, TGA, WMF, WBMP, JBG, J2K images. [zlib]
* [Dlib](https://github.com/davisking/dlib) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davisking/dlib?style=flat)](https://github.com/davisking/dlib/stargazers) :zap: - A modern C++11 machine learning, computer vision, numerical optimization, and deep learning toolkit. [Boost] [website](http://dlib.net/)
* [fpng](https://github.com/richgel999/fpng) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/richgel999/fpng?style=flat)](https://github.com/richgel999/fpng/stargazers) - Super fast C++ .PNG writer/reader. [Unlicense]
* [FreeImage](http://freeimage.sourceforge.net/) - An open source library that supports popular graphics image formats and others as needed by today's multimedia applications. [GPL2 or GPL3]
* [GD](https://github.com/libgd/libgd) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/libgd/libgd?style=flat)](https://github.com/libgd/libgd/stargazers) - GD Graphics Library, famously used in PHP for image loading/manipulation & thumbnail generation. [custom permissive license, requires mention in user docs] [website](http://libgd.github.io/)
* [DCMTK](http://dicom.offis.de/dcmtk.php.en) - DICOM Toolkit.
* [GDCM](http://gdcm.sourceforge.net/wiki/index.php/Main_Page) - Grassroots DICOM library.
* [ITK](http://www.itk.org/) - An open-source, cross-platform system for image analysis. [Apache2 from ITK 4.0]
* [Jpegli][https://github.com/google/jpegli] - an improved JPEG encoder and decoder implementation. [BSD-3-Clause]
* [Leptonica](https://github.com/DanBloomberg/leptonica) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DanBloomberg/leptonica?style=flat)](https://github.com/DanBloomberg/leptonica/stargazers) - Leptonica is an open source library containing software that is broadly useful for image processing and image analysis applications. [BSD-2-Clause] [website](http://leptonica.org/index.html)
* [libavif](https://github.com/AOMediaCodec/libavif) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AOMediaCodec/libavif?style=flat)](https://github.com/AOMediaCodec/libavif/stargazers) - Library for encoding and decoding .avif files. [BSD-2-Clause]
* [libfacedetection](https://github.com/ShiqiYu/libfacedetection) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ShiqiYu/libfacedetection?style=flat)](https://github.com/ShiqiYu/libfacedetection/stargazers) - Open source library for face detection in images. The face detection speed can reach 1500FPS. [BSD]
* [libjpeg-turbo](https://github.com/libjpeg-turbo/libjpeg-turbo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/libjpeg-turbo/libjpeg-turbo?style=flat)](https://github.com/libjpeg-turbo/libjpeg-turbo/stargazers) - A JPEG image codec that uses SIMD instructions to accelerate baseline JPEG encoding and decoding. [IJG & BSD-3-Clause & zlib] [website](https://libjpeg-turbo.org/)
* [libjxl](https://github.com/libjxl/libjxl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/libjxl/libjxl?style=flat)](https://github.com/libjxl/libjxl/stargazers) - JPEG XL image format reference implementation. [BSD-3-Clause]
* [libpng](https://github.com/pnggroup/libpng) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pnggroup/libpng?style=flat)](https://github.com/pnggroup/libpng/stargazers) - the reference library for use in applications that read, create, and manipulate PNG (Portable Network Graphics) raster image files. [libpng-2.0] [website](https://libpng.sourceforge.io/)

* [LodePNG](https://github.com/lvandeve/lodepng) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lvandeve/lodepng?style=flat)](https://github.com/lvandeve/lodepng/stargazers) - PNG encoder and decoder in C and C++. [Zlib]
* [Magick++](https://imagemagick.org/script/magick++.php) - ImageMagick program interfaces for C++. [Apache2]

## Internationalization

* [gettext](http://www.gnu.org/software/gettext/) - GNU 'gettext'. [GPL2]
* [IBM ICU](http://site.icu-project.org/) - A set of C/C++ and Java libraries providing Unicode and Globalization support. [ICU]
* [libiconv](http://www.gnu.org/software/libiconv/) - An encoding conversion library between different character encodings. [GPL]
* [simdutf](https://github.com/simdutf/simdutf) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/simdutf/simdutf?style=flat)](https://github.com/simdutf/simdutf/stargazers) - Unicode routines (UTF8, UTF16, UTF32): billions of characters per second using SSE2, AVX2, NEON, AVX-512. [Apache-2/MIT]
* [uni-algo](https://github.com/uni-algo/uni-algo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uni-algo/uni-algo?style=flat)](https://github.com/uni-algo/uni-algo/stargazers) - Unicode Algorithms Implementation for C/C++. [Unlicense or MIT]
* [utf8.h](https://github.com/sheredom/utf8.h) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sheredom/utf8.h?style=flat)](https://github.com/sheredom/utf8.h/stargazers) - Single header utf8 string functions for C and C++. [Unlicense]
* [utf8proc](https://github.com/JuliaStrings/utf8proc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JuliaStrings/utf8proc?style=flat)](https://github.com/JuliaStrings/utf8proc/stargazers) - A clean C library for processing UTF-8 Unicode data. [MIT]

## Inter-process communication

* [Apache Thrift](https://thrift.apache.org/) - Efficient cross-language IPC/RPC, works between C++, Java, Python, PHP, C#, and many more other languages. Originally developed by Facebook. [Apache2]
* [Boost.Interprocess](https://github.com/boostorg/interprocess) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boostorg/interprocess?style=flat)](https://github.com/boostorg/interprocess/stargazers) - Header-only Boost library that supports kernel-level shared memory and memory-mapped files, with in-built synchronization mechanisms (semaphores, mutexes, and more). [Boost] [website](https://boost.org/libs/interprocess)
* [bRPC](https://github.com/apache/brpc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apache/brpc?style=flat)](https://github.com/apache/brpc/stargazers) - bRPC is an Industrial-grade RPC framework using C++ Language, which is often used in high performance system such as Search, Storage, Machine learning, Advertisement, Recommendation etc. [Apache2] [website](https://brpc.apache.org/)
* [Cap'n Proto](https://github.com/capnproto/capnproto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/capnproto/capnproto?style=flat)](https://github.com/capnproto/capnproto/stargazers) - Fast data interchange format and capability-based RPC system. [MIT] [website](https://capnproto.org/)
* [eCAL](https://github.com/continental/ecal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/continental/ecal?style=flat)](https://github.com/continental/ecal/stargazers) - Pub/sub, client/server, C++/Python/C#, various message protocols (protobuf, capnproto ..). [Apache2] [website](http://www.ecal.io/)
* [gRPC](https://github.com/grpc/grpc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/grpc/grpc?style=flat)](https://github.com/grpc/grpc/stargazers) - A high performance, open source, general-purpose RPC framework. [BSD] [website](http://www.grpc.io/)
* [Ice](https://github.com/zeroc-ice/ice) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zeroc-ice/ice?style=flat)](https://github.com/zeroc-ice/ice/stargazers) - Comprehensive RPC framework with support for C++, C#, Java, JavaScript, Python and more. [GPLv2]
* [iceoryx](https://github.com/eclipse-iceoryx/iceoryx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eclipse-iceoryx/iceoryx?style=flat)](https://github.com/eclipse-iceoryx/iceoryx/stargazers) - True zero-copy inter-process communication framework for safety critical systems with bindings for C, Rust. Runs on Linux, QNX, Windows, Mac OS, FreeBSD. [Apache2] [website](https://iceoryx.io/)
* [libjson-rpc-cpp](https://github.com/cinemast/libjson-rpc-cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cinemast/libjson-rpc-cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/cinemast/libjson-rpc-cpp/stargazers) - JSON-RPC framework for C++ servers and clients. [MIT]
* [nanomsg](https://github.com/nanomsg/nanomsg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nanomsg/nanomsg?style=flat)](https://github.com/nanomsg/nanomsg/stargazers) - A simple high-performance implementation of several "scalability protocols". [MIT] [website](http://nanomsg.org/)
* [nng](https://github.com/nanomsg/nng) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nanomsg/nng?style=flat)](https://github.com/nanomsg/nng/stargazers) - nanomsg-next-generation, a light-weight brokerless messaging library. [MIT] [website](https://nanomsg.github.io/nng/)
* [rpclib](https://github.com/rpclib/rpclib) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rpclib/rpclib?style=flat)](https://github.com/rpclib/rpclib/stargazers) - A modern C++ msgpack-RPC server and client library. [MIT]
* [simple-rpc-cpp](https://github.com/pearu/simple-rpc-cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pearu/simple-rpc-cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/pearu/simple-rpc-cpp/stargazers) - A simple RPC wrapper generator to C/C++ functions. [BSD]
* [SRPC](https://github.com/sogou/srpc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sogou/srpc?style=flat)](https://github.com/sogou/srpc/stargazers) - A lightweight RPC system that supports multiple protocols and OpenTelemetry. [Apache2]
* [WAMP](http://wamp.ws/) - Provides RPC and pub/sub messaging patterns. (various implementations, various languages)
* [xmlrpc-c](http://xmlrpc-c.sourceforge.net/) - A lightweight RPC library based on XML and HTTP. [BSD]

## JSON

* [Boost.PropertyTree](https://github.com/boostorg/property_tree) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boostorg/property_tree?style=flat)](https://github.com/boostorg/property_tree/stargazers) - A property tree parser/generator that can be used to parse XML/JSON/INI/Info files. [Boost] [website](https://boost.org/libs/property_tree)

* [Glaze](https://github.com/stephenberry/glaze) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stephenberry/glaze?style=flat)](https://github.com/stephenberry/glaze/stargazers) - Extremely fast, in memory, JSON and interface library for modern C++. [MIT]
* [Jansson](https://github.com/akheron/jansson) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/akheron/jansson?style=flat)](https://github.com/akheron/jansson/stargazers) - C library for encoding, decoding and manipulating JSON data. [MIT]
* [jbson](https://github.com/chrismanning/jbson) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrismanning/jbson?style=flat)](https://github.com/chrismanning/jbson/stargazers) - jbson is a library for building & iterating BSON data, and JSON documents in C++14. [Boost]

* [Jsmn](https://github.com/zserge/jsmn) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zserge/jsmn?style=flat)](https://github.com/zserge/jsmn/stargazers) - A minimalistic JSON parser in C. [MIT]
* [json](https://github.com/nlohmann/json) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nlohmann/json?style=flat)](https://github.com/nlohmann/json/stargazers) :zap: - JSON for Modern C++. [MIT] [website](https://json.nlohmann.me)
* [JSON++](https://github.com/hjiang/jsonxx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hjiang/jsonxx?style=flat)](https://github.com/hjiang/jsonxx/stargazers) - A JSON parser in C++. [MIT]
* [json.cpp](https://github.com/jart/json.cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jart/json.cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/jart/json.cpp/stargazers) - a baroque JSON parsing / serialization library for C++. [Apache-2.0]
* [json.h](https://github.com/sheredom/json.h) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sheredom/json.h?style=flat)](https://github.com/sheredom/json.h/stargazers) - A simple one header/one source solution to parsing JSON in C and C++. [Unlicense]
* [json-build](https://github.com/lcsmuller/json-build) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lcsmuller/json-build?style=flat)](https://github.com/lcsmuller/json-build/stargazers) - C89 tiny zero-allocation JSON serializer. [MIT]
* [json-c](https://github.com/json-c/json-c) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/json-c/json-c?style=flat)](https://github.com/json-c/json-c/stargazers) - A JSON implementation in C. [MIT]
* [jsoncons](https://github.com/danielaparker/jsoncons) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/danielaparker/jsoncons?style=flat)](https://github.com/danielaparker/jsoncons/stargazers) - A C++ header-only library for JSON and JSON-like binary formats with JSONPointer, JSONPatch, JSONPath and JMESPath. [Boost]
* [JsonCpp](https://github.com/open-source-parsers/jsoncpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/open-source-parsers/jsoncpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/open-source-parsers/jsoncpp/stargazers) - A C++ library for interacting with JSON. [MIT]

## Logging

* [Abseil Logging](https://abseil.io/docs/cpp/guides/logging) - The Abseil Logging library provides facilities for writing log messages to stderr, files, or other sinks. [Apache-2.0]

* [G3log](https://github.com/KjellKod/g3log) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/KjellKod/g3log?style=flat)](https://github.com/KjellKod/g3log/stargazers) - Asynchronous logger with Dynamic Sinks. [PublicDomain]

* [haclog](https://github.com/MuggleWei/haclog) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MuggleWei/haclog?style=flat)](https://github.com/MuggleWei/haclog/stargazers) - An extremely fast plain C logging library. [MIT]

[BSD & Apache2]

* [lwlog](https://github.com/ChristianPanov/lwlog) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChristianPanov/lwlog?style=flat)](https://github.com/ChristianPanov/lwlog/stargazers) - Very fast synchronous and asynchronous C++17 logging library. [MIT]

## Math

* [Apophenia](https://github.com/b-k/apophenia) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/b-k/apophenia?style=flat)](https://github.com/b-k/apophenia/stargazers) - A C library for statistical and scientific computing. [GPL2]
* [Armadillo](https://gitlab.com/conradsnicta/armadillo-code) - Fast C++ library for linear algebra & scientific computing. [Apache2] [website](http://arma.sourceforge.net/)
* [autodiff](https://github.com/autodiff/autodiff) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/autodiff/autodiff?style=flat)](https://github.com/autodiff/autodiff/stargazers) - A modern, fast and expressive C++ library for automatic differentiation. [MIT] [website](https://autodiff.github.io)
* [blaze](https://bitbucket.org/blaze-lib/blaze) - high-performance C++ math library for dense and sparse arithmetic. [BSD]
* [Boost.Multiprecision](https://github.com/boostorg/multiprecision) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boostorg/multiprecision?style=flat)](https://github.com/boostorg/multiprecision/stargazers) - provides higher-range/precision integer, rational and floating-point types in C++, header-only or with GMP/MPFR/LibTomMath backends. [Boost] [website](https://boost.org/libs/multiprecision)
* [ceres-solver](http://ceres-solver.org/) - C++ library for modeling and solving large complicated nonlinear least squares problems from google. [BSD]
* [CGAL](https://github.com/CGAL/cgal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CGAL/cgal?style=flat)](https://github.com/CGAL/cgal/stargazers) - Collection of efficient and reliable geometric algorithms. [LGPL&GPL] [website](http://www.cgal.org/)
* [cml](https://github.com/demianmnave/CML) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/demianmnave/CML?style=flat)](https://github.com/demianmnave/CML/stargazers) - The configurable math library. [Boost]
* [CNL](https://github.com/johnmcfarlane/cnl/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/johnmcfarlane/cnl/?style=flat)](https://github.com/johnmcfarlane/cnl//stargazers) - A Compositional Numeric Library for C++. [Boost]
* [DirectXMath](https://github.com/microsoft/DirectXMath) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/microsoft/DirectXMath?style=flat)](https://github.com/microsoft/DirectXMath/stargazers) - An all inline SIMD C++ linear algebra library for use in games and graphics apps.
* [Dlib](https://github.com/davisking/dlib) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davisking/dlib?style=flat)](https://github.com/davisking/dlib/stargazers) :zap: - A modern C++11 machine learning, computer vision, numerical optimization, and deep learning toolkit. [Boost] [website](http://dlib.net/)
* [Eigen](http://eigen.tuxfamily.org/) - A high-level C++ library of template headers for linear algebra, matrix and vector operations, numerical solvers and related algorithms. [MPL2]
* [ExprTk](https://www.partow.net/programming/exprtk/) - The C++ Mathematical Expression Toolkit Library (ExprTk) is a simple to use, easy to integrate and extremely efficient run-time mathematical expression parser and evaluation engine. [MIT]
* [Fastor](https://github.com/romeric/Fastor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romeric/Fastor?style=flat)](https://github.com/romeric/Fastor/stargazers) - A lightweight high performance tensor algebra framework for modern C++. [MIT]
* [geo-utils-cpp](https://github.com/gistrec/geo-utils-cpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gistrec/geo-utils-cpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/gistrec/geo-utils-cpp/stargazers) - Header-only C++17 library for spherical lat/lng geometry: distance, bearing, area, point-in-polygon. [Apache2]
* [Geometric Tools](https://www.geometrictools.com) - C++ library for computing in the fields of mathematics, graphics, image analysis and physics. [Boost] [website](https://www.geometrictools.com)
* [GLM](https://github.com/g-truc/glm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/g-truc/glm?style=flat)](https://github.com/g-truc/glm/stargazers) - Header-only C++ math library that matches and inter-operates with OpenGL's GLSL math. [MIT] [website](https://glm.g-truc.net/)
* [GMTL](http://ggt.sourceforge.net/) - Graphics Math Template Library is a collection of tools implementing Graphics primitives in generalized ways. [GPL2]
* [GMP](https://gmplib.org/) - A C library for arbitrary precision arithmetic, operating on signed integers, rational numbers, and floating-point numbers. [LGPL3 & GPL2]
* [Klein](https://github.com/jeremyong/klein) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jeremyong/klein?style=flat)](https://github.com/jeremyong/klein/stargazers) - A fast, SIMD-optimized C++17 Geometric Algebra library for point, line, and plane projections, intersections, joins, rigid-body motion, and more. [MIT] [website](https://jeremyong.com/klein)
* [libfixmath](https://github.com/PetteriAimonen/libfixmath) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PetteriAimonen/libfixmath?style=flat)](https://github.com/PetteriAimonen/libfixmath/stargazers) - Cross Platform Fixed Point Maths Library. [MIT]
* [linalg.h](https://github.com/sgorsten/linalg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sgorsten/linalg?style=flat)](https://github.com/sgorsten/linalg/stargazers) - Single header, public domain, short vector math library for C++. [Unlicense]
* [MATIO](https://github.com/tbeu/matio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tbeu/matio?style=flat)](https://github.com/tbeu/matio/stargazers) -  MATLAB MAT File I/O Library. [BSD-2-Clause] [website](https://sourceforge.net/projects/matio/)
* [MatX](https://github.com/NVIDIA/MatX) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NVIDIA/MatX?style=flat)](https://github.com/NVIDIA/MatX/stargazers) - A GPU-accelerated C++17 numerical computing library with a MATLAB/Python-like syntax. [BSD 3-clause]
* [mexce](https://github.com/imakris/mexce) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/imakris/mexce?style=flat)](https://github.com/imakris/mexce/stargazers) - A single-header, dependency-free JIT compiler for scalar mathematical expressions that generates optimized x87 FPU machine code. [BSD]
* [MIRACL](https://github.com/CertiVox/MIRACL) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CertiVox/MIRACL?style=flat)](https://github.com/CertiVox/MIRACL/stargazers) - A Multiprecision Integer and Rational Arithmetic Cryptographic Library. [AGPL]
* [NumCpp](https://github.com/dpilger26/NumCpp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dpilger26/NumCpp?style=flat)](https://github.com/dpilger26/NumCpp/stargazers) - A templatized header only C++ implementation of the Python Numpy library. [MIT]
* [NumKong](https://github.com/ashvardanian/NumKong) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ashvardanian/NumKong?style=flat)](https://github.com/ashvardanian/NumKong/stargazers) - SIMD-accelerated distances, dot products, matrix ops, geospatial & geometric kernels for 16 numeric types. [Apache2] (previously named SimSIMD)
* [OMath](https://github.com/orange-cpp/omath) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orange-cpp/omath?style=flat)](https://github.com/orange-cpp/omath/stargazers) - Cross-platform modern general purpose math library written in C++23 that suitable for cheat/game development. [ZLIB]
* [muparser](https://beltoforion.de/en/muparser) - muParser is an extensible high performance math expression parser library written in C++. [MIT]
* [LibTomMath](https://github.com/libtom/libtommath) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/libtom/libtommath?style=flat)](https://github.com/libtom/libtommath/stargazers) - A free open source portable number theoretic multiple-precision integer library written entirely in C. [PublicDomain & WTFPL] [website](http://www.libtom.net/)
* [linmath.h](https://github.com/datenwolf/linmath.h) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/datenwolf/linmath.h?style=flat)](https://github.com/datenwolf/linmath.h/stargazers) - A lean linear math library, aimed at graphics programming. [WTFPL]
* [lp_solve](https://sourceforge.net/projects/lpsolve) - A library used to formulate and solve linear programming problems. [LGPL] [website](http://lpsolve.sourceforge.net)
* [OpenBLAS](https://github.com/xianyi/OpenBLAS) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xianyi/OpenBLAS?style=flat)](https://github.com/xianyi/OpenBLAS/stargazers) - An optimized BLAS library based on GotoBLAS2 1.13 BSD version. [BSD 3-clause] [website](http://www.openblas.net/)
* [PCG-rand](https://www.pcg-random.org/) - PCG is a family of simple fast space-efficient statistically good algorithms for random number generation. Unlike many general-purpose RNGs, they are also hard to predict. [Apache]
* [QuantLib](https://github.com/lballabio/quantlib) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lballabio/quantlib?style=flat)](https://github.com/lballabio/quantlib/stargazers) - A free/open-source library for quantitative finance. [Modified BSD] [website](http://quantlib.org/)

[Apache2] [website](https://sebsjames.github.io/maths/)

[BSD 3-clause] [website](https://xtensor-stack.github.io/xtensor)
* [universal](https://github.com/stillwater-sc/universal) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stillwater-sc/universal?style=flat)](https://github.com/stillwater-sc/universal/stargazers) - A C++14 header-only library implementing arbitrary posit arithmetic. The posit number system is a tapered floating point that is more efficient than IEEE floating point. Posits enable reproducible computational science. [MIT license]

## Memory Allocation

* [Boehm GC](https://github.com/ivmai/bdwgc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ivmai/bdwgc?style=flat)](https://github.com/ivmai/bdwgc/stargazers) - Conservative garbage collector for C and C++. [similar to X11] [website](http://www.hboehm.info/gc/)
* [C Smart Pointers](https://github.com/Snaipe/libcsptr) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Snaipe/libcsptr?style=flat)](https://github.com/Snaipe/libcsptr/stargazers) - Smart pointers for the (GNU) C programming language. [MIT]

* [jemalloc](https://github.com/jemalloc/jemalloc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jemalloc/jemalloc?style=flat)](https://github.com/jemalloc/jemalloc/stargazers) - General purpose malloc(3) implementation that emphasizes fragmentation avoidance and scalable concurrency support. [BSD] [website](http://jemalloc.net/)
* [memory](https://github.com/foonathan/memory) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/foonathan/memory?style=flat)](https://github.com/foonathan/memory/stargazers) - STL compatible C++ memory allocator library. [ZLib]

[MIT]
* [mimalloc](https://github.com/microsoft/mimalloc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/microsoft/mimalloc?style=flat)](https://github.com/microsoft/mimalloc/stargazers) - A compact general purpose allocator with excellent performance. [MIT]
* [rpmalloc](https://github.com/mjansson/rpmalloc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mjansson/rpmalloc?style=flat)](https://github.com/mjansson/rpmalloc/stargazers) - Cross platform lock free thread caching 16-byte aligned memory allocator implemented in C. [PublicDomain]
* [snmalloc](https://github.com/microsoft/snmalloc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/microsoft/snmalloc?style=flat)](https://github.com/microsoft/snmalloc/stargazers) - Message passing based high-performance allocator. [MIT]

* [tgc](https://github.com/orangeduck/tgc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/orangeduck/tgc?style=flat)](https://github.com/orangeduck/tgc/stargazers) - A tiny garbage collector for C written in \~500 LOC. [BSD]
* [Mesh](https://github.com/plasma-umass/Mesh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/plasma-umass/Mesh?style=flat)](https://github.com/plasma-umass/Mesh/stargazers) - A memory allocator that automatically reduces the memory footprint of C/C++ applications. [Apache-2.0]
* [rpmalloc](https://github.com/rampantpixels/rpmalloc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rampantpixels/rpmalloc?style=flat)](https://github.com/rampantpixels/rpmalloc/stargazers) - A public domain cross-platform lock-free thread-caching 16-byte aligned memory allocator. [PublicDomain]
* [TLSF](https://github.com/mattconte/tlsf) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattconte/tlsf?style=flat)](https://github.com/mattconte/tlsf/stargazers) - Two-Level Segregated Fit memory allocator, a general purpose dynamic memory allocator. [BSD]

[MIT]

## PDF

* [Poppler](https://poppler.freedesktop.org/) - Open-source multi-backend PDF rendering library based on the xpdf-3.0 code base. [GPLv2/GPLv3]
* [QPDF](https://github.com/qpdf/qpdf) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/qpdf/qpdf?style=flat)](https://github.com/qpdf/qpdf/stargazers) - A tool and C++ library for content-preserving transformations of PDF files. [Apache-2.0] [website](https://qpdf.sourceforge.io/)
